ACQUISITION of Lands
FORM VI

DECLARATION
[murhiz (ãiy) v©. 125, bghJ¥gâ¤ (¥Ã 2) Jiw, 9 br¥l«g® 2021, Mtâ 24,  
Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/646(b-1)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 74.60.35 hectares of land is required in 
the Ramakrishnapuram Village in Thisaiyanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely 
in Interlinking of Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project. Now, 
therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 74.60.35 hectares is under 
acquisition for the above said project in the Ramakrishnapuram Village in Thisaiyanvilai Taluk in 
Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

Total
74.60.35
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Office of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-4, Nanguneri and Office of the Executive Engineer, 
Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Tirunelveli on any working day.
	
SANDEEP SAXENA,
	
Additional Chief Secretary to Government

142	
Tamil  nadu  government  gazette  extraordinary
FORM VI
(See Rule 16)
DECLARATION
[murhiz (ãiy) v©. 126, bghJ¥gâ (¥Ã 2)¤ Jiw, 9 br¥l«g® 2021, Mtâ 24, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L 2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/646(b-2)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 42.83.65 hectares of land is required in the Moolakaraipatti part 1 and 2 Village in Nanguneri Taluk 
in Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely in Interlinking of Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar, Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Cannal Project. Now, therefore 
a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 42.83.65 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Moolakaraipatti part 1 
and 2 Village in Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-2, Nanguneri and O/o Executive Engineer, Public 
Works Department, Special Project Division, Ambasamudram on any working day.
	
SANDEEP SAXENA,
	
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

FORM VI
(See Rule 16)
DECLARATION
[murhiz (ãiy) v©. 128, bghJ¥gâ (¥Ã 2)¤ Jiw, 9 br¥l«g® 2021, Mtâ 24, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/646(b-3)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 8.63.71 hectares of land is required in the Kozhumadai Village in Cheranmahadevi Taluk 
in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely in Inter linking of Tamirabarani, Nambiyaru and Karumeniyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project. Now, 
therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 8.63.71 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Kozhumadai 
Village in Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Tirunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil. 
 Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
 A plan of the land may be inspected in the Office of the Land Acquisition Officer, O/o Special Tahsildar (L.A), River Linking Project, Unit I Ambasamudram 
at Cheranmahadevi and O/o Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Nanguneri on any working day.
	
SANDEEP SAXENA,
	
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

Tamil  nadu  government  gazette  extraordinary
FORM VI
(See Rule 16)
DECLARATION
[murhiz (ãiy)  v©.  129, bghJ¥gâ¤ (¥Ã 2) Jiw, 9 br¥l«g® 2021, Mtâ 24, Ãyt,  ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/646(b-4)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 54.75.91 hectares of land is required in the Moolakaraipatti Part 1 and 2 Village in Nanguneri Taluk 
in Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely in Interlinking of Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Cannal Project. Now, therefore 
a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 54.75.91 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Moolakaraipatti Part 1 
and 2 Village in Nanguneri Taluk in Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due 
to land acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines 
and minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being 
acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Office of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-2, Nanguneri and Office of the Executive Engineer, 
Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Ambasamuthiram on any working day.
	
SANDEEP SAXENA,
	
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.
